def pack_halves_any(x):
    x_i16=x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
    return ((x_i16[...,0::2]&0xFFFF)|((x_i16[...,1::2]&0xFFFF)<<16)).contiguous()

def a_onehot(r,k):
    x=torch.zeros((m.BATCH_SIZE,m.IN_FEATURES),device='cuda',dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    x[r,k]=1
    return m._pack_a(x)

def b_onehot(c,k):
    B=torch.zeros((m.N_TILES,m.K_TILES,64,4),device='cuda',dtype=torch.int32)
    if k < 4:
        l=c; s=k
    elif k < 8:
        l=32+c; s=k-4
    elif k < 12:
        l=c; s=4+(k-8)
    else:
        l=32+c; s=4+(k-12)
    lane_bf=torch.zeros((2,4),device='cuda',dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    lane_bf.view(-1)[s]=1
    B[0,0,l]=pack_halves_any(lane_bf).view(4)
    return B

y=torch.zeros((m.BATCH_SIZE,m.OUT_FEATURES),device='cuda',dtype=torch.bfloat16)
bias=torch.zeros((m.OUT_FEATURES,),device='cuda',dtype=torch.bfloat16)
for r,c,k in [(0,0,0),(1,0,0),(4,0,0),(0,1,0),(0,0,4),(0,0,8)]:
    A=a_onehot(r,k); B=b_onehot(c,k); y.zero_();
    m.gemm_bias_mfma_kernel[m._gemm_launch](A,B,bias,y)
    nz=(y[:32,:32]"'!=0).nonzero()

-def _launch():
-    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
 BATCH_SIZE = 1024
 IN_FEATURES = 8192
 OUT_FEATURES = 8192
 EPS = 1e-05
 DIVIDE_VALUE = 1.0
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
 
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_tiles = w_t.contiguous().view(K_TILES, K_STEP, N_TILES, 32).permute(2, 0, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    w_groups = w_tiles.view(N_TILES, K_TILES, K_STEP, 8, 4)
+    half0 = w_groups[:, :, 0:8, :, :].permute(0, 1, 3, 2, 4).contiguous()
+    half1 = w_groups[:, :, 8:16, :, :].permute(0, 1, 3, 2, 4).contiguous()
+    packed = _pack_halves_to_u32(torch.stack((half0, half1), dim=-2))
+    return packed.view(N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4).contiguous()
+

+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    wave_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    a_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+    b_lane = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_offset = S.convert((a_tile + kt * 64 + a_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    col = wave_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[col], S.f32)
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = wave_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    INVSTD: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),

+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((1,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    idx = S.block_id(0) * S.block_dim(0) + S.thread_id(0)

+        one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)

def pack_halves(x):
    x_i16=x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
    return ((x_i16[...,0::2]&0xFFFF)|((x_i16[...,1::2]&0xFFFF)<<16)).contiguous()

def direct_pack_b(w_t):
    w = w_t.t().contiguous()  # N,K
    out=torch.empty((m.N_TILES,m.K_TILES,64,4),device=w.device,dtype=torch.int32)
    wt = w.view(m.N_TILES,32,m.K_TILES,16).permute(0,2,1,3).contiguous() # Nt,Kt,32,16
    lo=torch.stack((wt[...,0:4], wt[...,8:12]), dim=-2)
    hi=torch.stack((wt[...,4:8], wt[...,12:16]), dim=-2)
    return torch.cat((pack_halves(lo), pack_halves(hi)), dim=2).contiguous()

torch.manual_seed(0)

+BLOCK_N = 64

+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32

+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP

+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))

+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()

+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_tiles = w_t.contiguous().view(K_TILES, K_STEP, N_TILES, 32).permute(2, 0, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    w_groups = w_tiles.view(N_TILES, K_TILES, K_STEP, 8, 4)
+    half0 = w_groups[:, :, 0:8, :, :].permute(0, 1, 3, 2, 4).contiguous()
+    half1 = w_groups[:, :, 8:16, :, :].permute(0, 1, 3, 2, 4).contiguous()
+    packed = _pack_halves_to_u32(torch.stack((half0, half1), dim=-2))
+    return packed.view(N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4).contiguous()

+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
 
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_tiles = w_t.contiguous().view(K_TILES, K_STEP, N_TILES, 32).permute(2, 0, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    w_groups = w_tiles.view(N_TILES, K_TILES, K_STEP, 8, 4)
+    half0 = w_groups[:, :, 0:8, :, :].permute(0, 1, 3, 2, 4).contiguous()
+    half1 = w_groups[:, :, 8:16, :, :].permute(0, 1, 3, 2, 4).contiguous()
+    packed = _pack_halves_to_u32(torch.stack((half0, half1), dim=-2))
+    return packed.view(N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4).contiguous()
+

+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),

+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE

+    warp_row = warp // 2

+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+    b_lane = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):

+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)

+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),

codex
The layout issue is isolated: the live `_pack_b` path in the file still uses the wrong K-major packing, even though the kernel itself is behaving correctly. I’m switching `_pack_b` to the verified N-major swizzle and tightening the weight cache to track the actual parameter storage.

+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))

+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16

 import torch.nn as nn
 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S
-SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951
 
-def _launch():
-    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
 BATCH_SIZE = 1024

 EPS = 1e-05
 DIVIDE_VALUE = 1.0
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    wave_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    a_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+    b_lane = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_offset = S.convert((a_tile + kt * 64 + a_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    col = wave_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[col], S.f32)
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = wave_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    INVSTD: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),

+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),

+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):

+    total = BATCH_SIZE * OUT_FEATURES
+    if idx < total:

-def _launch():
-    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
 BATCH_SIZE = 1024
 IN_FEATURES = 8192
 OUT_FEATURES = 8192
 EPS = 1e-05
 DIVIDE_VALUE = 1.0
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    wave_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    a_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+    b_lane = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_offset = S.convert((a_tile + kt * 64 + a_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+

 import torch.nn as nn
 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S
-SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951
 
-def _launch():
-    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
 BATCH_SIZE = 1024
 IN_FEATURES = 8192
 OUT_FEATURES = 8192
 EPS = 1e-05
 DIVIDE_VALUE = 1.0
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    wave_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    a_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+    b_lane = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_offset = S.convert((a_tile + kt * 64 + a_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    col = wave_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[col], S.f32)
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = wave_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    INVSTD: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((1,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    idx = S.block_id(0) * S.block_dim(0) + S.thread_id(0)
+    total = BATCH_SIZE * OUT_FEATURES
+    if idx < total:
+        row = idx // OUT_FEATURES
+        col = idx % OUT_FEATURES
+        v = (S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - MEAN[col]) * INVSTD[col]
+        v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+        v = (v + S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[0], S.f32)) / S.convert(DIVIDE_VALUE, S.f32)
+        one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
+        v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

import torch, importlib.util
path='/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p97/optimization_rounds/round1/output_model_new.py'
spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location('m', path)

spec.loader.exec_module(m)
torch.manual_seed(0)
model=m.ModelNew(m.IN_FEATURES,m.OUT_FEATURES).cuda().bfloat16()
x=torch.randn((m.BATCH_SIZE,m.IN_FEATURES),device='cuda',dtype=torch.bfloat16)

b=m._pack_b(w_t)
bias=model.matmul.bias.to(device='cuda',dtype=torch.bfloat16).contiguous()

ref=torch.nn.functional.linear(x, model.matmul.weight.to(device='cuda',dtype=torch.bfloat16), bias)
d=(y-ref).float().abs()

d2=(out-ref2).float().abs()
print('full max', d2.max().item(), 'mean', d2.mean().item())

+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    wave_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    a_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+    b_lane = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_offset = S.convert((a_tile + kt * 64 + a_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    col = wave_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[col], S.f32)
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = wave_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    INVSTD: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((1,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    idx = S.block_id(0) * S.block_dim(0) + S.thread_id(0)
+    total = BATCH_SIZE * OUT_FEATURES
+    if idx < total:
+        row = idx // OUT_FEATURES
+        col = idx % OUT_FEATURES
+        v = (S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - MEAN[col]) * INVSTD[col]
+        v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+        v = (v + S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[0], S.f32)) / S.convert(DIVIDE_VALUE, S.f32)
+        one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
+        v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)

+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    wave_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    a_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = warp_row * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+    b_lane = warp_col * WAVE_SIZE + lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_offset = S.convert((a_tile + kt * 64 + a_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    col = wave_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[col], S.f32)
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = wave_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    INVSTD: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((1,), S.bf16),

+    total = BATCH_SIZE * OUT_FEATURES

+        row = idx // OUT_FEATURES
+        col = idx % OUT_FEATURES

+        one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
+        v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

codex
The error is in the four-wave scaling, not the MFMA math. Wave-local A and B lane indices were being double-offset; I’m removing that extra `+ 64 * warp_*` term so each wave keeps the same 64-lane invariant and only the tile base shifts.

 import torch.nn as nn

 import substrate.language as S

-def _launch():
-    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
 BATCH_SIZE = 1024

 EPS = 1e-05
 DIVIDE_VALUE = 1.0
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+

+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),

+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32

+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)

+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = lane
+    b_lane = lane

+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)

+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]

+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+

 import torch.nn as nn
 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S
-SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951
 
-def _launch():
-    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
 BATCH_SIZE = 1024

 OUT_FEATURES = 8192
 EPS = 1e-05
 DIVIDE_VALUE = 1.0
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    wave_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    a_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = lane
+    b_lane = lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_offset = S.convert((a_tile + kt * 64 + a_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    col = wave_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[col], S.f32)
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = wave_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    INVSTD: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((1,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    idx = S.block_id(0) * S.block_dim(0) + S.thread_id(0)
+    total = BATCH_SIZE * OUT_FEATURES
+    if idx < total:
+        row = idx // OUT_FEATURES
+        col = idx % OUT_FEATURES
+        v = (S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - MEAN[col]) * INVSTD[col]

+        v = (v + S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[0], S.f32)) / S.convert(DIVIDE_VALUE, S.f32)
+        one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)

+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

 DIVIDE_VALUE = 1.0
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    wave_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    a_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = lane
+    b_lane = lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_offset = S.convert((a_tile + kt * 64 + a_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    col = wave_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[col], S.f32)
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = wave_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)

+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    wave_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    a_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = lane
+    b_lane = lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_offset = S.convert((a_tile + kt * 64 + a_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    col = wave_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[col], S.f32)
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = wave_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    INVSTD: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((1,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    idx = S.block_id(0) * S.block_dim(0) + S.thread_id(0)
+    total = BATCH_SIZE * OUT_FEATURES
+    if idx < total:
+        row = idx // OUT_FEATURES
+        col = idx % OUT_FEATURES
+        v = (S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - MEAN[col]) * INVSTD[col]
+        v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+        v = (v + S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[0], S.f32)) / S.convert(DIVIDE_VALUE, S.f32)
+        one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
+        v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

+def bn_apply_kernel(

+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),

+        v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[col], S.f32)

+        one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)

+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP

+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))

+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()

+@substrate.jit

+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = lane

+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]

The remaining delta is small enough that this looks like a numerics mismatch in the normalization tail. I’m matching the baseline formula more literally by storing `denom = sqrt(var + eps)` and dividing in the apply kernel instead of multiplying by an inverse.
apply patch

 import torch.nn as nn
 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S
-SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951
 
-def _launch():
-    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
 BATCH_SIZE = 1024
 IN_FEATURES = 8192
 OUT_FEATURES = 8192
 EPS = 1e-05
 DIVIDE_VALUE = 1.0
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    wave_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    a_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = lane
+    b_lane = lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_offset = S.convert((a_tile + kt * 64 + a_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    col = wave_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[col], S.f32)
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = wave_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+

+def bn_stats_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    DENOM: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),

         mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

+
         var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

-            d = S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32) - mean

+            var += delta * delta
+        var = var * inv_n
+
+        MEAN[col] = mean
+        DENOM[col] = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))

+
+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    DENOM: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((1,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    idx = S.block_id(0) * S.block_dim(0) + S.thread_id(0)
+    total = BATCH_SIZE * OUT_FEATURES
+    if idx < total:
+        row = idx // OUT_FEATURES
+        col = idx % OUT_FEATURES
+        v = (S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - MEAN[col]) / DENOM[col]
+        v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+        v = (v + S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[0], S.f32)) / S.convert(DIVIDE_VALUE, S.f32)
+        one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
+        v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    DENOM: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((1,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    idx = S.block_id(0) * S.block_dim(0) + S.thread_id(0)
+    total = BATCH_SIZE * OUT_FEATURES
+    if idx < total:
+        row = idx // OUT_FEATURES
+        col = idx % OUT_FEATURES
+        v = (S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - MEAN[col]) / DENOM[col]
+        v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+        v = (v + S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[0], S.f32)) / S.convert(DIVIDE_VALUE, S.f32)
+        one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
+        v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

 import torch.nn as nn
 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S
-SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951
 
-def _launch():
-    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
 BATCH_SIZE = 1024

 EPS = 1e-05
 DIVIDE_VALUE = 1.0
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    wave_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    a_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = lane
+    b_lane = lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_offset = S.convert((a_tile + kt * 64 + a_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+

+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[col], S.f32)
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = wave_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)

 import substrate.language as S

+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+

+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    DENOM: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((1,), S.bf16),

+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    wave_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    a_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = lane
+    b_lane = lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_offset = S.convert((a_tile + kt * 64 + a_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+

+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[col], S.f32)
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):

+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)

+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    wave_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    a_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = lane
+    b_lane = lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_offset = S.convert((a_tile + kt * 64 + a_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    col = wave_col_base + (lane % 32)
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[col], S.f32)
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = wave_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    DENOM: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((1,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    idx = S.block_id(0) * S.block_dim(0) + S.thread_id(0)
+    total = BATCH_SIZE * OUT_FEATURES
+    if idx < total:
+        row = idx // OUT_FEATURES
+        col = idx % OUT_FEATURES
+        v = (S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - MEAN[col]) / DENOM[col]
+        v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+        v = (v + S.convert(EXTRA_BIAS[0], S.f32)) / S.convert(DIVIDE_VALUE, S.f32)
+        one = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)
+        v = v * (one / (one + S.exp(-v)))
+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32

+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))

+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()

+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+

+    EXTRA_BIAS: S.Tensor((1,), S.bf16),

+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    A_PACK: S.Tensor((M_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    B_PACK: S.Tensor((N_TILES, K_TILES, 64, 4), S.u32),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    wave_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    wave_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    a_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+    b_shm_words = S.make_shared((THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 4), S.u32)
+
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A_PACK, M_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B_PACK, N_TILES * K_TILES * 64 * 16)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    a_tile = (wave_row_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    b_tile = (wave_col_base // 32) * K_TILES * 64
+    a_lane = lane
+    b_lane = lane
+
+    for kt in S.range(K_TILES):
+        a_offset = S.convert((a_tile + kt * 64 + a_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        b_offset = S.convert((b_tile + kt * 64 + b_lane) * 16, S.i32)
+        a_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_offset, 0)
+        b_vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_offset, 0)
+
+        a_shm_words[tid, 0] = a_vec[0]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 1] = a_vec[1]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 2] = a_vec[2]
+        a_shm_words[tid, 3] = a_vec[3]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 0] = b_vec[0]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 1] = b_vec[1]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 2] = b_vec[2]
+        b_shm_words[tid, 3] = b_vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag = S.view(a_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag = S.view(b_shm_words[tid], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+

+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[col], S.f32)
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):

+        Y[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx] + bias, S.bf16)

+def bn_apply_kernel(

 BATCH_SIZE = 1024
 IN_FEATURES = 8192

 DIVIDE_VALUE = 1.0
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+K_STEP = 16
+M_TILES = BATCH_SIZE // 32
+N_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // 32
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // K_STEP
+
+
+def _gemm_launch():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _vec_launch_1d(n, block=256):
+    return (((n + block - 1) // block, 1, 1), (block, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _pack_halves_to_u32(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_i16 = x.contiguous().view(torch.int16).to(torch.int32)
+    lo = x_i16[..., 0::2] & 0xFFFF
+    hi = (x_i16[..., 1::2] & 0xFFFF) << 16
+    return (lo | hi).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    x_tiles = x.contiguous().view(M_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 0:4], x_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((x_tiles[..., 4:8], x_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
+
+def _pack_b(w_t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    w_rows = w_t.t().contiguous()
+    w_tiles = w_rows.view(N_TILES, 32, K_TILES, K_STEP).permute(0, 2, 1, 3).contiguous()
+    lo_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 0:4], w_tiles[..., 8:12]), dim=-2)
+    hi_lanes = torch.stack((w_tiles[..., 4:8], w_tiles[..., 12:16]), dim=-2)
+    return torch.cat((_pack_halves_to_u32(lo_lanes), _pack_halves_to_u32(hi_lanes)), dim=2).contiguous()
+
